HTTPUserAgent returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "http.user_agent" semantic conventions. It represents the value of the [HTTP User-Agent]([https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#field.user-agent](https://www.rfc-editor.org/rfc/rfc9110.html#field.user-agent)) header sent by the client.

#### func [HostID](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L955)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#HostID "Go to HostID")

HostID returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "host.id" semantic conventions. It represents the unique host ID. For Cloud, this must be the instance_id assigned by the cloud provider. For non-containerized Linux systems, the `machine-id` located in `/etc/machine-id` or `/var/lib/dbus/machine-id` may be used.

#### func [MessagingConsumerID](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L2826)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#MessagingConsumerID "Go to MessagingConsumerID")

func MessagingConsumerID(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

MessagingConsumerID returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "messaging.consumer.id" semantic conventions. It represents the identifier for the consumer receiving a message. For Kafka, set it to `{messaging.kafka.consumer.group} - {messaging.kafka.client_id}`, if both are present, or only `messaging.kafka.consumer.group`. For brokers, such as RabbitMQ and Artemis, set it to the `client_id` of the client consuming the message.

#### func [MessagingKafkaMessageKey](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L2936)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#MessagingKafkaMessageKey "Go to MessagingKafkaMessageKey")

MessagingKafkaMessageKey returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "messaging.kafka.message.key" semantic conventions. It represents the message keys in Kafka are used for grouping alike messages to ensure they're processed on the same partition. They differ from `messaging.message.id` in that they're not unique. If the key is `null`, the attribute MUST NOT be set.

#### func [MessagingMessagePayloadCompressedSizeBytes](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L2535)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#MessagingMessagePayloadCompressedSizeBytes "Go to MessagingMessagePayloadCompressedSizeBytes")

#### func [MessagingMessagePayloadSizeBytes](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L2527)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#MessagingMessagePayloadSizeBytes "Go to MessagingMessagePayloadSizeBytes")

func MessagingMessagePayloadSizeBytes(val [int](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#int)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

MessagingMessagePayloadSizeBytes returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "messaging.message.payload_size_bytes" semantic conventions. It represents the (uncompressed) size of the message payload in bytes. Also use this attribute if it is unknown whether the compressed or uncompressed payload size is reported.

func OTelLibraryName(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

OTelLibraryName returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "otel.library.name" semantic conventions. It represents the deprecated, use the `otel.scope.name` attribute.

#### func [OTelLibraryVersion](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1997)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#OTelLibraryVersion "Go to OTelLibraryVersion")

OTelLibraryVersion returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "otel.library.version" semantic conventions. It represents the deprecated, use the `otel.scope.version` attribute.

#### func [OTelScopeName](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1952)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#OTelScopeName "Go to OTelScopeName")

OTelScopeName returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "otel.scope.name" semantic conventions. It represents the name of the instrumentation scope - (`InstrumentationScope.Name` in OTLP).

#### func [OTelScopeVersion](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1959)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#OTelScopeVersion "Go to OTelScopeVersion")

func OTelScopeVersion(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

OTelScopeVersion returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "otel.scope.version" semantic conventions. It represents the version of the instrumentation scope - (`InstrumentationScope.Version` in OTLP).

#### func [OTelStatusDescription](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L794)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#OTelStatusDescription "Go to OTelStatusDescription")

OTelStatusDescription returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "otel.status_description" semantic conventions. It represents the description of the Status if it has a value, otherwise not set.

#### func [PeerService](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L1486)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#PeerService "Go to PeerService")

func PeerService(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

PeerService returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "peer.service" semantic conventions. It represents the [`service.name`](../../resource/semantic_conventions/README.md#service) of the remote service. SHOULD be equal to the actual `service.name` resource attribute of the remote service if any.

#### func [ProcessCommand](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1590)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessCommand "Go to ProcessCommand")

func ProcessCommand(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessCommand returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.command" semantic conventions. It represents the command used to launch the process (i.e. the command name). On Linux based systems, can be set to the zeroth string in `proc/[pid]/cmdline`. On Windows, can be set to the first parameter extracted from `GetCommandLineW`.

#### func [ProcessCommandArgs](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1611)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessCommandArgs "Go to ProcessCommandArgs")

func ProcessCommandArgs(val ...[string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessCommandArgs returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.command_args" semantic conventions. It represents the all the command arguments (including the command/executable itself) as received by the process. On Linux-based systems (and some other Unixoid systems supporting procfs), can be set according to the list of null-delimited strings extracted from `proc/[pid]/cmdline`. For libc-based executables, this would be the full argv vector passed to `main`.

#### func [ProcessCommandLine](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1600)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessCommandLine "Go to ProcessCommandLine")

func ProcessCommandLine(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessCommandLine returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.command_line" semantic conventions. It represents the full command used to launch the process as a single string representing the full command. On Windows, can be set to the result of `GetCommandLineW`. Do not set this if you have to assemble it just for monitoring; use `process.command_args` instead.

#### func [ProcessExecutableName](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1572)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessExecutableName "Go to ProcessExecutableName")

func ProcessExecutableName(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessExecutableName returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.executable.name" semantic conventions. It represents the name of the process executable. On Linux based systems, can be set to the `Name` in `proc/[pid]/status`. On Windows, can be set to the base name of `GetProcessImageFileNameW`.

#### func [ProcessExecutablePath](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1581)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessExecutablePath "Go to ProcessExecutablePath")

func ProcessExecutablePath(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessExecutablePath returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.executable.path" semantic conventions. It represents the full path to the process executable. On Linux based systems, can be set to the target of `proc/[pid]/exe`. On Windows, can be set to the result of `GetProcessImageFileNameW`.

#### func [ProcessOwner](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1618)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessOwner "Go to ProcessOwner")

ProcessOwner returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.owner" semantic conventions. It represents the username of the user that owns the process.

#### func [ProcessPID](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1556)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessPID "Go to ProcessPID")

ProcessPID returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.pid" semantic conventions. It represents the process identifier (PID).

#### func [ProcessParentPID](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1563)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessParentPID "Go to ProcessParentPID")

ProcessParentPID returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.parent_pid" semantic conventions. It represents the parent Process identifier (PID).

#### func [ProcessRuntimeDescription](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1678)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessRuntimeDescription "Go to ProcessRuntimeDescription")

func ProcessRuntimeDescription(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessRuntimeDescription returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.runtime.description" semantic conventions. It represents an additional description about the runtime of the process, for example a specific vendor customization of the runtime environment.

#### func [ProcessRuntimeName](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1662)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessRuntimeName "Go to ProcessRuntimeName")

func ProcessRuntimeName(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessRuntimeName returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.runtime.name" semantic conventions. It represents the name of the runtime of this process. For compiled native binaries, this SHOULD be the name of the compiler.

#### func [ProcessRuntimeVersion](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1670)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#ProcessRuntimeVersion "Go to ProcessRuntimeVersion")

func ProcessRuntimeVersion(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

ProcessRuntimeVersion returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "process.runtime.version" semantic conventions. It represents the version of the runtime of this process, as returned by the runtime without modification.

#### func [RPCJsonrpcErrorCode](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L3361)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#RPCJsonrpcErrorCode "Go to RPCJsonrpcErrorCode")

RPCJsonrpcErrorCode returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "rpc.jsonrpc.error_code" semantic conventions. It represents the `error.code` property of response if it is an error response.

#### func [RPCJsonrpcErrorMessage](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L3368)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#RPCJsonrpcErrorMessage "Go to RPCJsonrpcErrorMessage")

func RPCJsonrpcErrorMessage(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

RPCJsonrpcErrorMessage returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "rpc.jsonrpc.error_message" semantic conventions. It represents the `error.message` property of response if it is an error response.

#### func [RPCJsonrpcRequestID](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L3354)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#RPCJsonrpcRequestID "Go to RPCJsonrpcRequestID")

func RPCJsonrpcRequestID(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

RPCJsonrpcRequestID returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "rpc.jsonrpc.request_id" semantic conventions. It represents the `id` property of request or response. Since protocol allows id to be int, string, `null` or missing (for notifications), value is expected to be cast to string for simplicity. Use empty string in case of `null` value. Omit entirely if this is a notification.

#### func [RPCJsonrpcVersion](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L3344)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#RPCJsonrpcVersion "Go to RPCJsonrpcVersion")

func RPCJsonrpcVersion(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

RPCJsonrpcVersion returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "rpc.jsonrpc.version" semantic conventions. It represents the protocol version as in `jsonrpc` property of request/response. Since JSON-RPC 1.0 does not specify this, the value can be omitted.

#### func [RPCMethod](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/trace.go#L3237)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#RPCMethod "Go to RPCMethod")

RPCMethod returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "rpc.method" semantic conventions. It represents the name of the (logical) method being called, must be equal to the $method part in the span name.

#### func [WebEngineDescription](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1921)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#WebEngineDescription "Go to WebEngineDescription")

func WebEngineDescription(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

WebEngineDescription returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "webengine.description" semantic conventions. It represents the additional description of the web engine (e.g. detailed version and edition information).

#### func [WebEngineName](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1906)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#WebEngineName "Go to WebEngineName")

func WebEngineName(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

WebEngineName returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "webengine.name" semantic conventions. It represents the name of the web engine.

#### func [WebEngineVersion](https://github.com/open-telemetry/opentelemetry-go/blob/v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0/resource.go#L1913)[¶](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/semconv/v1.18.0#WebEngineVersion "Go to WebEngineVersion")

func WebEngineVersion(val [string](https://pkg.go.dev/builtin#string)) [attribute](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute).[KeyValue](https://pkg.go.dev/go.opentelemetry.io/otel@v1.40.0/attribute#KeyValue)

WebEngineVersion returns an attribute KeyValue conforming to the "webengine.version" semantic conventions. It represents the version of the web engine.
